 1980 ke chunaav main phir is seat ko choudhary rajendra prasad yadav ne chin liya
 Chaudhary Mahavir Prasad Yadav of Congress won the Madhepura seat in the 1984 elections
 1989 main janata dal ne is seat se choudhary ramendra kumaar yadav ravi ko utaara or unhone jeet kaa paracham laharaaya
 After this, Sharad Yadav, who played a leading role in JP movement, chose Madhepura as his political work place
 1991 or 1996 ke chunaav main janata dal ke tikat par yahaan se jitkar sharad yadav loksabhaa pahunche

 What is the Economic Survey? - The Economic Survey is an annual document of the Ministry of Finance in which the government presents a review of the economy
 -parampara ke mutabik is aadhikarik report ko salanaa bajet se ek din pehle sansad ke donon sadanon main pesh kiya jaataa he
 - Economic Survey estimates the growth rate of economy in the coming year

 - Through the government report, the current state of the economy is presented to the country

 - Economic survey calculates the prospects of the economy from short to medium term

" ve log desh ke liye apni chintaa nahin karte or hameshaa desh kii seva main tatpar rahete hai

 moonak nahar or haryana se rajdhani ko milane vaale pani se jude maamle main sunwaayee ke dauraan shuukravaar ko jal board ne court ko bataaya ki dilli main abhi keval 55 fisadi aria main siver system he
 The remaining 45 percent of the sewer will be put in place by 2031
 jal board kii baat sunne ke baad naaraaz court ne kaha ki 'tab tak to rajdhani gande pani ke talab main tabdeel ho jaaegi
 The High Court is hearing a public interest litigation filed on the issue of water from the Moonak Canal and Haryana to the capital
 court ne chintaa jaahir karte hue kaha aise ilaakon kaa kya hoga jahaan siver system nahin he
 The court directed the Delhi Water Board to present its next hearing in the court regarding the sewer system
 court ne jal board se poocha kii vah report pesh kar bataaen kirajdhanimen kitna sivej paidaa hota he
 What is done with this? isamen se kitna pani saaf hone ke baad istemaal kiya jaataa he or dilli kii siver treetment system kii kshamta kitni he
 The court asked the water board to either work on it themselves or take the help of an expert to survey what is the problem with sewerage
 unka samaadhaan kaise kiya jaae or is par apni kaam karne kii yojana taiyaar karen
 During the hearing, the court also expressed concern that 500 million gallons of sewage is being dumped into the river every day
 vahiin, rojaanaa paidaa hone vaale 900 million galen siver main se keval 400 million galen siver treetment plant main pahunch rahaa he
 While the plant has a capacity of 604 million gallons
 hai court main yachikakarta ne dilli jal board or dilli sarkaar ko siver ke pani ko saaf kar use pine laayak or baaki ke kaamon main istemaal karne ke liye istemaal main laane laayak banane kaa nirdesh dene ke liye maang kii he
 The case will be next heard on 21 October

 in mauton ke kaaran gujarat main sampradayik hinsa fail gai
 Shocking the government's hopes of improving the country's financial standing, the international credit rating agency S&P has maintained the country's financial standing at 'bbb-negative' levels, with the economy expected to remain similarly stable next year
 is
 agency ne rajkoshiya sthiti kii kamajori kaa hawala dete desh kii saakh ke maujuuda str se unche str par pahunchane kii sambhaavna se inkaar kiya he
 The government on Wednesday slammed global rating agencies for not upgrading India's sovereign rating
 sarkaar ne kaha ki itane sudhaar ke baad bhi bharat kii reating main sudhaar na karne vaali agenciyon ko aatmvishleshan karne kii jarurat he, kyonki vaishvik str par niveshkon kaa maananaa he ki bharat kii reating ko ‘kam’ yaa nichle str par rakhaa gaya he
 Economic Affairs Secretary Shaktikanta Das said that the government will continue to follow the path of economic reforms and policies
 das ne kaha, "yadi reating main sudhaar nahin hota he, to yah aisa maamla he jo hamen adhik pareshaan nahin karata he
 This is a question that needs to be introspected by ratings
 " S&P Global Ratings said in a statement, "it is from this stable scenario that there is a balance between India's external frontal strength and inclusive policy making tradition and low per capita income and weak public financial position
" " isamen kaha gaya he, ""anumaan vyakt karne ke hamaare maujuuda mandandon ke aadhaar par paridrishy se yah sanket miltaa he ki is saal or agle saal ke liye bharat kii reating main badlaav kii koi ummid nahin he
 "'BBB negative' rating is the lowest rating of the investable categories
 esendpy kaa kahana he ki us par credit reating ko badhaane kaa dabaav tabhi banegaa jab sudhaaron se sarkaar kii vittiya sthiti main ullekhneey sudhaar dikhaai de or sarkaar kaa saamaanya rin jidipi ke 60 pratishat se neeche aa jaae
 At present, the domestic debt of the Government of India has reached 69 percent of GDP
 agency ne kaha he ki niti nirmaan main sudhaar ke baavjood vittiya ghate, baari rin boj or nimna prati vyakti aay kii chintaa lagaataar badi he
 It says that if the reforms do not go ahead, the Monetary Policy Committee setting the rate of interest is not able to meet the inflation target and disappoints the growth rate, then the pressure to reduce the rating will increase again
 esendpy ne kaha he bharat kii bahya taralata sthiti main ummid se zyada kamajori aane se bhi usapar reating ko kam karne kaa dabaav badhegaa
 The rating agency expects India's economic growth rate to be 7 in 2016
 9 pratishat rahegi
 During this period, the current account deficit is 1 of the gross domestic product (GDP)
 4 pratishat rahegaa
 The agency also hopes that the Reserve Bank will achieve the inflation target of five percent by March 2017
 esendpy ne isse pehle sitambar 2014 main bharat kii reating ko badhaakar nakaaratmak se sthir kar diya tha
 The agency says that India's rating has reflected India's strong position on the external front and the improvement in monetary credibility
 agency ne kaha he ki bharat ke majboot loktantric sansthana or swatantra media uski natiyon ko sthirataa or vishwasaneeyata ko badhaate hai
 While praising the government's success in getting the GST Bill passed and building consensus among political parties for it, the rating agency said it could bring comprehensive tax reforms in the first half of 2017
 agency ne anya sudhaaron main vyavsaayik maahaul ko behatar bananaa, shram bazaar main lacheelaapan badhanaa or urja kshetra main sudhaaron ko ahm bataaya he
 The comments bharat kii reating badhane kii aashaaon par agency ne kaha ki 2016 main bharat kii 1,700 dollars kii prati vyakti nimna jidipi rahaa he
 However, India's growth rate is higher than its counterpart and it is growing
 reating agency ko 2016 main bharat kii jidipi vruddhi dar 7
 It is expected to remain 9 percent and an average 8 percent increase between 2016-2018
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) vahiin, sarkaar ne buudhvaar ko bharat kii sovrain reating kaa unnayan na karne ke liye vaishvik reating agenciyon ko aade haath liya
 The government said that even after so much improvement, agencies that do not improve India's rating need to introspect, as investors globally believe that India's rating is kept at 'low' or low
 aarthik maamalon ke sachiv shaktikant das ne kaha ki sarkaar aarthik sudhaar or nitiyon kii raah par aage chalanaa jari rakhegi
 Das said, "if the rating does not improve, it is a matter that does not bother us much
 yah aisa sawaal he jiske jawaab main reating karne waalon ko aatmvishleshan karne kii jarurat he
 " esendpy global reating ne ek vaktavy main kaha he, "is sthir paridrishy se hi bharat kii bahari morche par majbootee tathaa samaveshi nitinirmaan parampara or nimna prati vyakti aay tathaa kamjor saarvajanik vittiya sthiti ke bich santulan bana hua he
 "it adds," "the scenario, based on our current criteria for projecting estimates, indicates that there is no hope of a change in India's ratings for this year and next year
" " ‘bibibi rinatmak’ reating nivesh yogya shreniyon kii sabase nichali darje kii reating he
 The S&P says that it will be pressurized to raise the credit rating only if the reforms show a significant improvement in the government's financial condition and the government's normal debt falls below 60 percent of GDP
 bharat sarkaar kaa is samay gharelu rin jidipi kaa 69 pratishat tak pahunch chukaa he
 The agency said that despite improvement in policy formulation, concerns about fiscal deficit, heavy debt burden and low per capita income have steadily increased
 uskaa kahana he ki yadi sudhaar aage nahin badhate hai, byaaj dar tay karne vaali maudrik niti samiti mudrasphiti lakshya ko hasil nahin kar paati he or vruddhi dar niraash karti he to reating kam karne kaa dabaav us par phir se bad jayega
 The S&P has said that due to a higher than expected weakness in India's external liquidity position, there will be pressure on it to lower the rating
 reating agency ko ummid he ki 2016 main bharat kii aarthik vruddhi dar 7
 Will be 9 percent
 is dauraan chaalu khate kaa ghaataa sakal gharelu utpaada (jidipi) kaa 1
 Will remain 4 percent
 agency ko yah bhi ummid he ki rigerv bank march 2017 tak paanch pratishat ke mudrasphiti lakshya ko hasil kar legaa
 S&P had earlier raised India's rating to stable from negative in September 2014
 agency kaa kahana he ki usne bharat kii jo reating di he usase bharat ke bahari morche par majbootee sthiti or maudrik saakh main aayaa sudhaar parilakshith hota he
 The agency has stated that India's strong democratic institutions and independent media enhance stability and credibility to its policies
 sarkaar dwaara jiesti vidheyak ko paarit karaane or raajnneetik dalon ke bich iske liye aam sahmati kaayam karne main safal rahane kii prashansa karte hue reating agency ne kaha he ki isse varsh 2017 kii pehali chamahi main vyapak kar sudhaar amal main aa sakate hai
 Among other reforms, the agency has called for improving the business environment, increasing flexibility in the labor market and reforms in the energy sector
 tippaniyan On hopes of India's rating rising, the agency said that India had a low GDP per capita of $ 1,700 in 2016
 haalanki bharat kii vruddhi dar uske samakaksh duusare deshon se adhik rahi he or yah aage bad rahi he

 Swasti means welfare or Mars
 isi prakaar swastik kaa arth hota he - kalyaan yaa mangal karne vaala
 Swastik is a special figure, which is made before the beginning of any work
 mana jaataa he ki , yah chaaron dishaao se shubh or mangal ko aakarshith karata he
 Since it is kept in the beginning of work and Mars, it is also considered as the form of Lord Ganesha
 mana jaataa he ki iske prayog se sampannataa, samruddhi or ekaagratha kii prapti hoti he
 The worship in which the swastika is not used, the worship is not able to have its effect for a long time
 swaastik kaa vaigyanik mahatv kya he?- sahi tareeke se bane hue swastik se dher sari sakaaratmak urja nikalati he- yah urja vastu yaa vyakti kii raksha , suraksha karne main madadgaar hoti he- swastik kii urja kaa agar ghar , aspataal yaa dainik jivan main prayog kiya jaay to vyakti rogamukt or chintaa mukt rah saktaa he- galat tareeke se prayog kiya gaya swastik bhayankar samasyaayen bhi de saktaa haiswastik ke prayog ke sahi niyam kya hai?- swaastik kii rekhaaen or kone bilkul sahi hone chahie- bhuulakar bhi ulate swastik kaa nirmaan or prayog na karen- laal or pile rang ke swastik hi sarvshereshth hote hai- agar swastik ko dhaaran karnaa he to iske gole ke andar dhaaran karankis prakaar karen swaastik kaa prayog?- jahaan jahaan vaastu dosha ho , yaa ghar ke mukhya dwaar par laal rang kaa swastik banaaen- puja ke sthaan, padhai ke sthaan or vaahan main apane saamne , swastik banaaen- ekaagratha ke liye , sone yaa chaandi main bana hua swastik , laal dhaage main dhaaran karen- electronic upkarnon par chote chote swastik lagane se, ve jaldi karaab nahin hote The time between Christmas and New Year is special for the stock markets around the world

 What is the Uniform Civil Code? Uniform Civil Code means uniform law for every citizen in the country

 - muslim mahilaon kii sthiti behatar hogi
 - The image of India is that of a secular country

 samvidhan ke anuchhed 44 main uniform civil code kaa paksh liya gaya he, lekin ye diarective princepal hai
